  cycle            Tells the bot to cycle the current songs in the queue
  recommend        Allow the bot to add up to 5 songs to the queue to have in...
  music            Returns the current status of the Music Bot
  youtube          Adds a Song for the Bot to Play
  viewplaylist     Views the songs of a playlists
  radio            Enables Radio Mode
  loop             Plays the current song again
  leave            Leaves the Join chat

  unmuteall        Unmutes ALL muted players

13 Sep 2017 03:13:16 : Botfuzzy77 Living Quarters, updates, Wertfuzzy77#0274, v.1.3.1 Update @​everyone 
**Enhancements**
- `;afk` now has a nicer formatted message when alerting you that someone is afk
- `;afk` now also shows how long the person has been afk for

**Pokegame Balancing**
*People seem to be getting too much free xp from ;train, so I am nerfing `;train` a little bit*
- Increased `;train`'s to an hour (from 30 minutes)
- Reduced the average XP given from `;train` by around 12%
- Boosted the damage that bosses take by 15%, so keep hunting those bosses!
- Increased the damage of each STAB move by 2%
